< Text>
I think better tasting than Panda Express for fast food Chinese food.
Reasonable fast service and decent sit-down tables and some side options like soup and BBQ Pork Buns and egg rolls and cold drinks. The soup comes with the 3-item combo, a bit pricier Chinese food than fast food like Panda Express.

<time>1522970834312<//time><resp>None</resp><gmapID>0x808fb6d7d4b2a343:0xc7a9638dd9faaca9<//gmapID><UserId.>100871700591441784888</UserId.>< review>
A tasty take on express Chinese takeout. One of the few places that offers decent chow fun as an option other than fried rice or chow mein. They have remodeled the inside so the interior is very snazzy and clean. They do use some of the public tables to shell veggies but it's usually not very crowded. They have a couple of outdoor tables.

It is in a densely populated strip mall with a ton of stores. This is one of a couple of restaurants. Parking can be problematic because it is a very busy parking lot but they do have a ton of spaces.

Their food is quite tasty and they've been here a long time! Their best express table dish isntheir black pepper chicken.<//review>

There was a minor delay for ordering, but the gal working came out and took my order to keep me from having to wait too long. I like the mango smoothie, and the pretzel wrapped hot dog was quite good. The delay was waiting for the dogs to cook, apparently those sell pretty quick and take a little time to cook. I like the drive through, there are two windows, but it could make a decent sit down place on another location. Service was great, fast  considering that the pretzels were fresh made.<//Review>

<resp>None<//resp><review>I had a very strange experience at this place.

I pull into their drive through, and get greeted by a very alarmed looking woman. "Hi" she says,

"Hi, I'd like a plain salted pretzel and a water" I replied.

She then proceeds to look at me with an expression on her face like I'm clinically insane. "You want a what???" she says. "A salted pretzel and a water?" I reply.

She pauses and continues to look at me with an expression of complete and utter confusion. "A salted...pretzel?" she says. "Yes....?" I reply.

"Ok, and you want water? What kind of water to you want?" she says. Now I'm the one looking at her with a look of utter confusion.

"A bottle?" she asks. I nod in the affirmative. I'm then quickly given a bagged pretzel and water, and drive off.

It's difficult to explain. It definitely wasn't that she didn't hear me at first. It's that she was genuinely shocked and deeply confused that I was ordering a salted pretzel. From "The Pretzel Place."

The pretzel itself was okay? Not outstanding, but not stale and gross. I don't want to go out of my way to knock businesses like this. The world needs more drive-through pretzel stands, believe me.

But for the owner...maybe share this review with your team and talk about customer service fundamentals with them? And make sure they're okay??</review>< Name>

Reheating: Do not reheat in microwave! You must do cast-iron/pan in oven at 350 -- it is extremely good reheated this way.

<text>A pizza is as it‚Äôs, just a pizza for everyone. It‚Äôs affordable, it‚Äôs quick, it‚Äôs tasty, it really is delicious. The pie style is thin, with a proper load of ingredients on top. < Review>
It's all about the value here.  For $2.75--yes $2.75!--I had a fine Margherita pizza that was very tasty and fresh out of the oven.  Granted it's not quite up to Delifina around the corner, but for 1/5 the price it is seriously worth eating!  The staff is super nice and almost all French folks with their charming accents.  They offer the requisite shakers of oregano, hot pepper and Parmesan, plus real knives and forks for civilized eating.  Ironically, my Diet Coke costs almost exactly as much as my pizza!  (They gotta make some profit somewhere.) But this concept is a winner.<//Review>

I went to this location on Tuesday with my boyfriend to try out the food since it seemed like a really good place to eat Mexican food at. We were completely wrong. We ordered online, there was a 35 minute wait for our food, which we did not mind. When the 35 minutes came by, I went into the store. I was not greeted by anyone so I went up to the girl who seems to be helping people with online orders. I told her that I was there to pick up food and gave her my name. She just kept looking at me and then stared at my phone. I asked her if she needed the email for confirmation and with attitude she said yes. She then wrote down my name and told me to wait outside. I waiting for 10 minutes after the 35 minutes I was required to wait. I went inside and since she was not around, I waited for her to come back. Before talking to her, the client she was talking to said he had been waiting for an hour already. I asked her "how much longer until I receive my order" and she just stared at me and nodded and walked away. Meanwhile she went to help another client to look for his order, he mentioned that he was waiting for an hour and 30 minutes which seems ridiculous for the fact that it was a pick up order and people in the drive thru and walking into the store were getting their orders faster. When I got my order, the quesadilla I ordered was no even cooked throughly. The cheese was not melted at all and was still chunky, also full of grease. I also ordered the tacitos and the plate was a mess. It did not even seem like an effort was made to put it together. We also ordered a surf and turf bowl which was missing the carne asada. The ceviche was leaking which made the tostadas soggy. This was one of my worse customer experiences at your location and they should properly  train their employees because our money is paying their bills.< /review>

< review>
Each time I place an advanced telephone order or order in person, there is always a long wait. Whether they are busy or not, average waiting period is a minimum of 20 minutes.

Keep in mind that all their proteins - whether it would be fish, carne asada, al pastor, or lengua are cooked in advance. All the cooks need to do is assemble these proteins for tacos, burritos, fries, etc.

So why the slow speed??? Both Alhambra locations are extremely slow despite my numerous complaints to the managers.

If you don't mind the lengthy wait or chaos at the restaurant, then Baja Cali is your place!<//review>

<Text>I've tried the aguachiles tostada, fish tacos, carne asada tacos, chicken tacos, potatoe tacos, shrimp cocktail, asada sope, chicken sope, horchata, and cucumber water. I love the fish tacos the best. Their meat isn't lean, so if you don't like eating fat, you'll have to pick it out of your food like I do. If you like spicy foods try the aguachiles and get that cucumber water with mint and chia seeds. It's the most refreshing drink! A good meatless option are the potatoe tacos, they're delicious.
If you go on a Tuesday, the line goes all the way outside and it was way too crowded to eat inside because the fish tacos are 99cents each. On Thursdays the meat tacos are 99cents each.

*UPDATE* Feb 2018
I recently also tried the barbacoa tacos, pi√±a agua fresca and strawberry agua fresca. All three were really good.  I gave it another go with the carne asada and chicken and ordered sopes but their meat still isn't clean so I couldn't eat 80% of it. I even ASK before ordering if their meat has "cuero". The cashier thought I meant skin and had me ask one of the cooks and he said it was clean (but it wasn't like always) -.- so I'll stick to the fish tacos and barbacoa!

*UPDATE* March 2018
Extremely lean meat in my sope!!! I ordered a carne asada sope and I FINALLY got no fat with my meat, it was delicious! I hope they keep it up!!!</Text>< Rating>

I found that other items on the menu were closer to average. The pastor and carne asada tacos I had were both relatively tasty, but the meat itself didn't seem to be of great quality. Their condiment and sides bar is extensive, with radishes, onions, and large banana peppers available.

The service is just okay, and we had to wait a decent amount of time for our food.
